The Psalms

   BOOK I


Psalm 1


-1  0 
WEB:Psalms:1:1:Verse:0WEBPsalms 1  1  Blessed is the man who doesn't walk in the counsel of the wicked,
   nor stand in the way of sinners,
   nor sit in the seat of scoffers;
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:1:2:Meta:1WEBPsalms 1  2 1:Footnote "Yahweh" is God's proper Name, sometimes rendered "LORD" (all caps) in other translations.-1  1 
WEB:Psalms:1:2:Verse:1WEBPsalms 1  2  but his delight is in Yahweh's law.
   On his law he meditates day and night.
 0  1 
WEB:Psalms:1:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 1  3  He will be like a tree planted by the streams of water,
   that brings forth its fruit in its season,
   whose leaf also does not wither.
   Whatever he does shall prosper.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:1:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 1  4  The wicked are not so,
   but are like the chaff which the wind drives away.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:1:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 1  5  Therefore the wicked shall not stand in the judgment,
   nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:1:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 1  6  For Yahweh knows the way of the righteous,
   but the way of the wicked shall perish.

 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:1:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  1  Why do the nations rage,
   and the peoples plot a vain thing?
 0  0

WEB:Psalms:2:2:Verse:2WEBPsalms 2  2  The kings of the earth take a stand,
   and the rulers take counsel together,
   against Yahweh, and against his Anointed, saying,
 0  2 
WEB:Psalms:2:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  3  "Let's break their bonds apart,
   and cast their cords from us."
 0  0

WEB:Psalms:2:4:Verse:3WEBPsalms 2  4  He who sits in the heavens will laugh.
   The Lord will have them in derision.

   and terrify them in his wrath:

    0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  7  I will tell of the decree.

   Today I have become your father.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  8  Ask of me, and I will give the nations for your inheritance,
   the uttermost parts of the earth for your possession.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:9:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  9  You shall break them with a rod of iron.

 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:10:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  10  Now therefore be wise, you kings.
   Be instructed, you judges of the earth.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:11:Verse:0WEBPsalms 2  11  Serve Yahweh with fear,
   and rejoice with trembling.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:2:12:Meta:4WEBPsalms 2  12 4:Footnote or, Kiss the son-1  4 
WEB:Psalms:2:12:Verse:4WEBPsalms 2  12  Give sincere homage to the Son, lest he be angry, and
      you perish in the way,
   for his wrath will soon be kindled.
   Blessed are all those who take refuge in him.


Psalm 3

A Psalm by David, when he fled from Absalom his son.


 0  4 
WEB:Psalms:3:1:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  1  Yahweh, how my adversaries have increased!
   Many are those who rise up against me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:2:Meta:5WEBPsalms 3  2 5:Footnote The Hebrew word rendered "God" is "Elohim."-1  5 
WEB:Psalms:3:2:Verse:5WEBPsalms 3  2  Many there are who say of my soul,
   "There is no help for him in God."
Selah.
 0  5 
WEB:Psalms:3:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  3  But you, Yahweh, are a shield around me,
   my glory, and the one who lifts up my head.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  4  I cry to Yahweh with my voice,
   and he answers me out of his holy hill.
Selah.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  5  I laid myself down and slept.
   I awakened; for Yahweh sustains me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  6  I will not be afraid of tens of thousands of people
   who have set themselves against me on every side.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  7  Arise, Yahweh!
   Save me, my God!
For you have struck all of my enemies on the cheek bone.
   You have broken the teeth of the wicked.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:3:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 3  8  Salvation belongs to Yahweh.
   Your blessing be on your people.
Selah.

   Have mercy on me, and hear my prayer.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:2:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  2  You sons of men, how long shall my glory be turned into dishonor?

Selah.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  3  But know that Yahweh has set apart for himself him who is godly:
   Yahweh will hear when I call to him.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  4  Stand in awe, and don't sin.
   Search your own heart on your bed, and be still.
Selah.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  5  Offer the sacrifices of righteousness.
   Put your trust in Yahweh.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  6  Many say, "Who will show us any good?"
   Yahweh, let the light of your face shine on us.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  7  You have put gladness in my heart,
   more than when their grain and their new wine are increased.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:4:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 4  8  In peace I will both lay myself down and sleep,
   for you, Yahweh alone, make me live in safety.


Psalm 5

For the Chief Musician, with the flutes. A Psalm by David.


 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:1:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  1  Give ear to my words, Yahweh.
   Consider my meditation.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:2:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  2  Listen to the voice of my cry, my King and my God;
   for to you do I pray.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  3  Yahweh, in the morning you shall hear my voice.
   In the morning I will lay my requests before you, and will watch
      expectantly.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  4  For you are not a God who has pleasure in wickedness.
   Evil can't live with you.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  5  The arrogant shall not stand in your sight.
   You hate all workers of iniquity.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  6  You will destroy those who speak lies.
   Yahweh abhors the bloodthirsty and deceitful man.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  7  But as for me, in the abundance of your loving kindness I will
      come into your house.
   I will bow toward your holy temple in reverence of you.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  8  Lead me, Yahweh, in your righteousness because of my enemies.
   Make your way straight before my face.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:9:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  9  For there is no faithfulness in their mouth.
   Their heart is destruction.
   Their throat is an open tomb.
   They flatter with their tongue.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:10:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  10  Hold them guilty, God.
   Let them fall by their own counsels;
Thrust them out in the multitude of their transgressions,
   for they have rebelled against you.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:11:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  11  But let all those who take refuge in you rejoice,
   Let them always shout for joy, because you defend them.
Let them also who love your name be joyful in you.
    0  0 
WEB:Psalms:5:12:Verse:0WEBPsalms 5  12  For you will bless the righteous.
Yahweh, you will surround him with favor as with a shield.

WEB:Psalms:6:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  4  Return, Yahweh. Deliver my soul,

WEB:Psalms:6:5:Meta:6WEBPsalms 6  5 6:Footnote Sheol is the place of the dead.-1  6

 0  6 
WEB:Psalms:6:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  6  I am weary with my groaning.
   Every night I flood my bed.
   I drench my couch with my tears.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:6:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  7  My eye wastes away because of grief.
   It grows old because of all my adversaries.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:6:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  8  Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity,
   for Yahweh has heard the voice of my weeping.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:6:9:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  9  Yahweh has heard my supplication.
   Yahweh accepts my prayer.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:6:10:Verse:0WEBPsalms 6  10  May all my enemies be ashamed and dismayed.
   They shall turn back, they shall be disgraced suddenly.

Cush, the Benjamite.

   ripping it in pieces, while there is none to deliver.

   if there is iniquity in my hands,

WEB:Psalms:7:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 7  4  if I have rewarded evil to him who was at peace with me
   (yes, if I have delivered him who without cause was my adversary),

WEB:Psalms:9:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 9  3  When my enemies turn back,

WEB:Psalms:9:9:Verse:0WEBPsalms 9  9  Yahweh will also be a high tower for the oppressed;

WEB:Psalms:9:16:Verse:0WEBPsalms 9  16  Yahweh has made himself known.

WEB:Psalms:10:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 10  4  The wicked, in the pride of his face,
   has no room in his thoughts for God.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:10:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 10  5  His ways are prosperous at all times.
   He is haughty, and your laws are far from his sight.

    0  0 
WEB:Psalms:10:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 10  6  He says in his heart, "I shall not be shaken.

Psalm 38

A Psalm by David, for a memorial.


 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:1:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  1  Yahweh, don't rebuke me in your wrath,
   neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:2:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  2  For your arrows have pierced me,
   your hand presses hard on me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:3:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  3  There is no soundness in my flesh because of your indignation,
   neither is there any health in my bones because of my sin.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:4:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  4  For my iniquities have gone over my head.
   As a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:5:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  5  My wounds are loathsome and corrupt,
   because of my foolishness.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:6:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  6  I am pained and bowed down greatly.
   I go mourning all day long.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:7:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  7  For my waist is filled with burning.
   There is no soundness in my flesh.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:8:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  8  I am faint and severely bruised.
   I have groaned by reason of the anguish of my heart.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:9:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  9  Lord, all my desire is before you.
   My groaning is not hidden from you.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:10:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  10  My heart throbs.
   My strength fails me.
   As for the light of my eyes, it has also left me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:11:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  11  My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my plague.
   My kinsmen stand far away.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:12:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  12  They also who seek after my life lay snares.
   Those who seek my hurt speak mischievous things,
   and meditate deceits all day long.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:13:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  13  But I, as a deaf man, don't hear.
   I am as a mute man who doesn't open his mouth.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:14:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  14  Yes, I am as a man who doesn't hear,
   in whose mouth are no reproofs.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:15:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  15  For in you, Yahweh, do I hope.
   You will answer, Lord my God.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:16:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  16  For I said, "Don't let them gloat over me,
   or exalt themselves over me when my foot slips."
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:17:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  17  For I am ready to fall.
   My pain is continually before me.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:18:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  18  For I will declare my iniquity.
   I will be sorry for my sin.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:19:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  19  But my enemies are vigorous and many.
   Those who hate me without reason are numerous.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:20:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  20  They who also render evil for good are adversaries to me,
   because I follow what is good.
 0  0 
WEB:Psalms:38:21:Verse:0WEBPsalms 38  21  Don't forsake me, Yahweh.
